###################################################################################


#------------------------'Definitions'---------------------------------#

Path Simple:	The netting event of the tracked address that receives the contracts happens at the begining

Path Complex:	The netting event of the tracked address that receives the contracts happens after the contracts are
				opened or keep open contracts at the end date

------------------------------------------------------
